Myopia Dataset: Chinese Youth (2018–2025)

This dataset includes a sample of 500 children per year (aged 4–19) in China. This dataset is published as a free resource for students conducting research or for anyone who might find it useful. All information from this dataset are reserved to its rightful owner. ©2025 First published: July/09/2019 Last edited: March/02/2025
